function rp_anim(e,s,u,f,t,tm) // graceful expansion/collapse function
{
if (!e) return;
g = (f > t) ? 'c' : 'e';
var st = new Date().getTime(),
tmr = setInterval( function() {
var stp = Math.min( 1, ( new Date().getTime() - st ) / tm );
if (g === 'e') {
if (!e.s) { e.setAttribute(s, f + stp * (t - f)) } else { e[s] = f + stp * (t - f) }
if (e.style[s]) e.style[s] = (f + stp * (t - f)) + u;
} else {
if (!e.s) { e.setAttribute(s, f - stp * (f - t)) } else { e[s] = f - stp * (f - t) }
if (e.style[s]) e.style[s] = (f - stp * (f - t)) + u;
}
if ( stp === 1 ) clearInterval( tmr );
}, 25 );
if (!e.s) { e.setAttribute(s, f) } else { e[s] = f }
if (e.style[s]) { e.style[s] = ( f + u ) } else { e.style[s] = f + u }
}
rp_resize = function(sz,id)
{
var d, w, sh, h;
w = sz.substring(0, sz.indexOf('x'));
h = sz.substring(sz.indexOf('x') + 1, sz.length);
d = document.getElementById(id);
if (d.getBoundingClientRect().height) {
sh = d.getBoundingClientRect().height; // for modern browsers
} else {
sh = d.offsetHeight; // for oldIE
}
if (!d.width) { d.setAttribute('width', parseInt(w)) } else { d.width = parseInt(w) }
if (d.style.width) d.style.width = parseInt(w)+'px';
rp_anim(d, 'height', 'px', sh, h, 500);
}
</script>

<!-- GeoRiot code -->
<script type="text/javascript">
$(document).ready(function () {
// READ THIS!!
// START OF REQUIRED CHANGES
// you MUST change this value to one for your georiot account TSIDs
var tsid = 3658;
// END OF REQUIRED CHANGES
// DO NOT MODIFY BELOW THIS LINE
convertToGeoRiotLinks(tsid);
// convertToGeoRiotLinks(3658) is also called in the galleries: loadMPU
});
function convertToGeoRiotLinks(tsid) {
var numberOfLinks = document.links.length;
var currentLinkIndex = 0;
for (currentLinkIndex = 0; currentLinkIndex < numberOfLinks; currentLinkIndex++) {
var currentLink = document.links[currentLinkIndex];
var linkType = getLinkType(currentLink.href);
if (linkType == "apple" || linkType == "amazon") {
currentLink.href = "http://target.georiot.com/Proxy.ashx?TSID=" + tsid + "&GR_URL=" + encodeURIComponent(currentLink.href);
} else if (linkType == "linkshare" || linkType == "tradedoubler" || linkType == "dgmperf") {
var itunesUrl = extractItunesLinkFromAffiliateUrl(currentLink, linkType);
if (itunesUrl != "") {
currentLink.href = "http://target.georiot.com/Proxy.ashx?TSID=" + tsid + "&GR_URL=" + itunesUrl;
}
} else continue;
}
}
function extractItunesLinkFromAffiliateUrl(currentLink, linkType) {
if (currentLink.href.indexOf("?") > 0) {
var arrParams = currentLink.href.split("?");
var arrURLParams = arrParams[1].split("&");
var arrParamNames = new Array(arrURLParams.length);
var arrParamValues = new Array(arrURLParams.length);
var i = 0;
for (i = 0; i < arrURLParams.length; i++) {
var sParam = arrURLParams[i].split("=");
arrParamNames[i] = sParam[0];
if (sParam[1] != "") {
arrParamValues[i] = sParam[1];
if (linkType == "tradedoubler" && arrParamNames[i] == "url") {
return arrParamValues[i];
} else if (linkType == "linkshare" && arrParamNames[i] == "RD_PARM1") {
return arrParamValues[i];
} else if (linkType == "dgmperf" && arrParamNames[i] == "u") {
return arrParamValues[i];
}
} else arrParamValues[i] = "";
}
}
return "";
}
/* Returns link type: unknown, amazon, apple, linkshare, dgm, tradedoubler
*/
function getLinkType(currentLinkHref) {
var appleRegex = /itunes.apple.com\/\S+id[0-9]+/i;
var tradeDoublerRegex = /clk[uk]*\.tradedoubler\.com\S*\?\S*url=[https%3A%2F%2F|http%3A%2F%2F]*\itunes\.apple\.com/i;
var linkshareRegex = /click\.linksynergy\.com\S*?\S*RD_PARM1=[https%3A%2F%2F|https%253A%252F%252F|http%253A%252F%252F|http%3A%2F%2F]*\itunes\.apple\.com/i;
var dgmPerfRegex = /t.dgm-au.c\S+\?+\S*u=[https%3A%2F%2F|http%3A%2F%2F|https%253A%252F%252F|http%253A%252F%252F]*\itunes\.apple\.com/i;
var amazonRegex = /\.amazon\./;
var amazonLocalRegex = /local\.amazon\./;
if (currentLinkHref.indexOf("target.georiot.com") > 0 || currentLinkHref.indexOf("geni.us") > 0) {
return "unknown";
}
if (appleRegex.test(currentLinkHref)) return "apple";
else if (tradeDoublerRegex.test(currentLinkHref)) return "tradedoubler";
else if (linkshareRegex.test(currentLinkHref)) return "linkshare";
else if (dgmPerfRegex.test(currentLinkHref)) return "dgmperf";
else if (amazonRegex.test(currentLinkHref) && !amazonLocalRegex.test(currentLinkHref)) return "amazon";
else return "unknown";
};
$(".esi-gallery-rightarrow").click(function() {
console.log('runnit')
});
</script>

var valParentID = $(this).parents('.commentBlock').first().attr('id');
var event = {
commentText: valCommentText,
side: '',
parentID: valParentID,
errorContainerClass : "errorReply"
};

categoryID: params.categoryID,
streamID: params.streamID,
commentText: event.commentText,
parentID: event.parentID,
callback: function(response) {
if(response.errorCode == 0) {
$('.replyFormClone').html('<p class="successMsg">Your comment has been successfully submitted</p>');
} else {
}
}
});
return false;
});
} else {
gigya.accounts.showScreenSet({screenSet:'Short-login-web2'});
}
});

<script type="text/javascript">
$(function() {
$("#simpleSearch-5054704 .field").autocomplete({
source: ajaxCall ,
delay: 2000.00,
close: function(event, ui) {
$("#simpleSearch-5054704 .field").autocomplete("option", "delay", 500.00);
},
select: function(event, ui) {
var articleId = ui.item.id;
openLink('http://www.independent.co.uk/eceRedirect?articleId=' + articleId, '_self');
}
});
});
function ajaxCall(request, response) {
var iChars = "!@#$%^&*()+=-[]\\\';,./{}|\":<>?~_";
var term = $.trim(request.term.toLowerCase());
var wordCount = term.split(" ").length;
if (term.length > 0 && iChars.indexOf(term.charAt(0)) == -1) {
var param = "(" + term + "*) publication:(ind) state:(published) contenttype:(news)";
$.ajax({
url: "/ind/ewf-servlet/search/",
data: {q:param , rows:5, wt:'json'},
cache: true,
dataType: 'json',
success: function(json) {
var responseCount = json.response.docs.length;
if (json != null && responseCount > 0) {
response($.map(json.response.docs, function(article) {
return {label: article.title, value: article.title, id: article.objectid}
}));
}
else{
$("#simpleSearch-5054704 .field").autocomplete("close");
}
if (wordCount > 1 && responseCount == 0) {
param = "(" + term + ") publication:(ind) state:(published) contenttype:(news)";
$.ajax({
url: "/ind/ewf-servlet/search/",
data: {q:param , rows:5, wt:'json'},
cache: true,
dataType: 'json',
success: function(json) {
var responseCount = json.response.docs.length;
if (json != null && responseCount > 0) {
response($.map(json.response.docs, function(article) {
return {label: article.title, value: article.title, id: article.objectid}
}));
}
}
})
}
}
})
}
else if (term.length > 0 && iChars.indexOf(term.charAt(0)) != -1) {
$("#simpleSearch-5054704 .field").autocomplete("close");
alert("Search word should not start with !@#$%^&*()+=-[]\\\';,./{}|\":<>?~_");
}
}
</script>

<script>
$(document).ready(function () {
$.ajax({
dataType: "json",
url: "http://i100.independent.co.uk/feed/",
error: function (e) {
console.log(e);
},
success: function (e) {
$.each(e['articles'], function (e, t) {
var imageUrl = '';
for (var i=0;i<t.images.length;i++) {
if (t.images[i].type == 'thumbnail') {
imageUrl = t.images[i].url;
break;
}
}
$("#i100-list").append("<div class='i100-item card-" + t.category + "'><div class='i100-img'><a href='"+t.displayURL+"?utm_source=indy&utm_medium=top5&utm_campaign=i100' target='_blank'><img src='"+ imageUrl +"' width='70px'/></a></div><div class='i100-txt'><div class='i100-byline'><a href='"+t.displayURL +"?utm_source=indy&utm_medium=top5&utm_campaign=i100' target='_blank'><span class='i100-count'>"+(e+1)+"</span><a href='"+t.displayURL +"?utm_source=indy&utm_medium=top5&utm_campaign=i100' target='_blank'><span class='i100-headline'>"+ t.headline +"</span></a></div>");
});
}
});
});
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
$(function() {
$("#simpleSearch-5054704 .field").autocomplete({
source: ajaxCall ,
delay: 2000.00,
close: function(event, ui) {
$("#simpleSearch-5054704 .field").autocomplete("option", "delay", 500.00);
},
select: function(event, ui) {
var articleId = ui.item.id;
openLink('http://www.independent.co.uk/eceRedirect?articleId=' + articleId, '_self');
}
});
});
function ajaxCall(request, response) {
var iChars = "!@#$%^&*()+=-[]\\\';,./{}|\":<>?~_";
var term = $.trim(request.term.toLowerCase());
var wordCount = term.split(" ").length;
if (term.length > 0 && iChars.indexOf(term.charAt(0)) == -1) {
var param = "(" + term + "*) publication:(ind) state:(published) contenttype:(news)";
$.ajax({
url: "/ind/ewf-servlet/search/",
data: {q:param , rows:5, wt:'json'},
cache: true,
dataType: 'json',
success: function(json) {
var responseCount = json.response.docs.length;
if (json != null && responseCount > 0) {
response($.map(json.response.docs, function(article) {
return {label: article.title, value: article.title, id: article.objectid}
}));
}
else{
$("#simpleSearch-5054704 .field").autocomplete("close");
}
if (wordCount > 1 && responseCount == 0) {
param = "(" + term + ") publication:(ind) state:(published) contenttype:(news)";
$.ajax({
url: "/ind/ewf-servlet/search/",
data: {q:param , rows:5, wt:'json'},
cache: true,
dataType: 'json',
success: function(json) {
var responseCount = json.response.docs.length;
if (json != null && responseCount > 0) {
response($.map(json.response.docs, function(article) {
return {label: article.title, value: article.title, id: article.objectid}
}));
}
}
})
}
}
})
}
else if (term.length > 0 && iChars.indexOf(term.charAt(0)) != -1) {
$("#simpleSearch-5054704 .field").autocomplete("close");
alert("Search word should not start with !@#$%^&*()+=-[]\\\';,./{}|\":<>?~_");
}
}
</script>
